9! ##########################################################################
10 SUBROUTINE lima_read_xker_raccs (KACCLBDAS,KACCLBDAR,KND, &
11 PALPHAS,PNUS,PALPHAR,PNUR,PESR,PBS,PBR,PCS,PDS,PFVELOS,PCR,PDR, &

17!!**** * * - initialize the kernels for the rain-snow accretion process
18!!
19!! PURPOSE
20!! -------
21!! The purpose of this routine is to initialize the kernels PKER_RACCSS,

32!! None
33!!
34!!

41!! Book2 of documentation ( routine READ_XKER_RACCS )
42!!
43!! AUTHOR
44!! ------
45!! J.-P. Pinty * Laboratoire d'Aerologie*

49!! Original 09/04/96
50!!
51!-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
52!
53!* 0. DECLARATIONS
54! ------------
55!
56!* 0.2 Declarations of arguments :
57!
58!
59INTEGER, INTENT(OUT) :: KND
60INTEGER, INTENT(INOUT) :: KACCLBDAS,KACCLBDAR
61REAL, INTENT(OUT) :: PALPHAS
62REAL, INTENT(OUT) :: PNUS
